< Review>
My family has owned a time share at Laguna Surf for over 30 years, we're original owners. It has been kept up and managed wonderfully over the years, and the current management staff is probably the best they've ever had. The rooms are very comfortable, and they all include fully functional kitchens, complete with pots, pans, plates, and cutlery. The units facing the ocean offer some of the best views in Laguna. Laguna Surf is also ideally located within walking distance from most of the best spots in town. We go every year and have no intentions of selling.< /Review>

For an ocean front property the beds are smaller than a queen & the mattresses feel as if they were leftover from 1960 they are so worn, lumpy & have such poor support. And the sheets have been used so much they have nubs on them. I was & have been appalled by this over the 8 years I‚Äôve been coming here w/ my boyfriend now husband who invested in this condo years before me. This time I was disgusted that one of the pillowcases smelled of BO but because we came after 5 pm no one is ever here to help w/ bedding. And since we had to commute back & forth based on our work schedules we kept coming after 5 & so never got to get a new pillowcase. We love Laguna & the locale is great & beach access is super but the beds & sheets are so old & used you would think you were in a 1 Star hotel. The location is perfect, just a short walk away from the downtown part of Laguna. The rooms are a good size with two bathrooms a master bedroom and a pull out Murphy bed from the wall. < Review>
I have had had two experiences with Alfred Matthews service dept. and both have been solid. I have a 1997 Suburban 4wd with a 454/7.4l. These vehicles have a few things that need attention after 160K miles. A mechanic named Glen knew these older truck styles and all their idiosyncrasies, he took care of the proportion-valve/rear brake issues without the usual diagnosis of fixing everything but the problem like most places would do. He knew exactly what needed to be done and fixed it. Even on an aftermarket part, he was able to find a fin or a slot or some weird thing on a rotor that was causing an ongoing mystery pull to the left. He used the shop resources(lots of 100k machines the standard shop won't have) to remedy the problem and solved a world a headache. I notice some bad reviews here, and believe me I'm the first one to blast any shop that I feel was just experimenting with my money, but these guys did good by me so I'm guessing those may have come from a different era of personnel. I've been there twice and I'll go there next time I have any issues with my burb.<//Review>

The food was amazing and the staff was very respectable.  Hands down 5 stars. Had a very good meal and nice experience @Mia last night. Is a nice neighborhood trattoria with very friendly people that own and run it. The food was very good, the grilled octopus with asparagus sauce, the tonnarelli cacio e Pepe pasta dish was superb and then for main courses the lamb chops and the prime beef were also very good. Wonderful!

We started with an Insalata Mista, dressed with a nice perky balsamic vinaigrette. We had three pasta dishes and all were excellent: Rigatoni Amatriciana, Tonnarelli Cacio e Pepe (the pasta is fresh not dried) and Spaghetti alla Carbonara. Dessert was also excellent: fresh Strawberry Gelato, Tiramisu and Cannoli Siciliani. We finished with Espresso and Cappuccino which both had incredible crema (foam).

There are so many delicious choices on their menu that I can hardly wait to return for another wonderful meal.< /Review>

< text>
The donuts had a fresh taste to them that I had not experienced in a while.
The Apple fritters were not over fried and hard as it n most places. The cinnamon roll was moist and fluffy.
The pastries were not over glazed. The blueberry doughnuts were tasty and the kids went crazy over the chocolate glazed ones.
It's a small place I discovered when visiting the pho place next door.
It's a bit pricier than most doughnut shops in the area, but worth it.
Don't wait too long, the close at 1.< /text>

< Review>
Beautiful moderate to easy hike. Spring has lots of stunning wildflowers and this year the river is up and flowing rapidly. Lots of little trail offshoots to explore. Easy enough for kiddos. Lots of other people, but not overwhelming. Dog on leash friendly. Restaurant and cafe nearby outside of park if you want to get breakfast or lunch before or after your hike.<//Review>

<Name>joshua Quevedo< /Name>< Date>
1476980214541<//Date>
<Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Great place to hike and explore. If you don't cross the covered bridge from the old jail house side there is a trail you can hike. You can enjoy the beautiful scenery while you and the family get some experience. There is also a spot where you can cliff job. If you cross the covered bridge there is a trail as well, one that is not so family friendly that will take you all the way along to someone's property. You can cross the river from either side by jumping from rock to rock when the water level is low enough. I have done this multiple times with friends. It's a beautiful and great time. It's a must see if you are visiting or a local to the surrounding area.< /review>

<gmapID>0x808ff8def7032093:0x70261143bbb3dbcb<//gmapID><userid>105167985360598472369<//userid>< Review>
I've had some good hair colorings at Fusion 3 in Livermore, but I am not going back to any of these three salons. Half a year ago, I expressly asked for a new talent hair coloring and then added on a haircut that day. I wasn't warned that the woman cutting my hair was experienced talent, so I was surprised at the end by the bill. Yesterday at the Brentwood salon, I was going to be 15 minutes late to a hair appointment, and while I do not like lateness, this was still around rush hour, so I hoped they would be understanding. After just 10 minutes beyond my scheduled time, I got a call saying that my hair colorist was already starting on another client. So apparently, she only had allotted 10 minutes to sit me down, get me a cup of coffee, mix the color and apply the coloring to my hair????? Sounds unlikely. I was offered the choice of getting experienced talent & going home with wet hair or else rescheduling. I opted for switching to another salon. I cannot imagine that other clients are never 10-15 minutes late, but it seems Fusion 3 lacks flexibility to juggle their appointments.< /Review>

<Rate>5< /Rate><review>I got my tattoo from Mars, or cloudsolid on Instagram, and it was all around perfect.
First of all, he is overall super nice and chill. He can draw anything you suggest and he will get it exactly how you imagine it. Then throughout the whole process he makes sure you‚Äôre comfortable, relaxed and able to keep going. During the tattoo you can just chat and have a nice convo, or if you need to relax he will just focus on the tattoo and not even mind, so he is great for all those introverted snd extroverted people. He is also very nice about working with your budget. You can tell him how much you have and he will completely work around that.
Secondly, just his tattoo machine is the best because it is so quite and feels super nice compared to other tattoo machines. For me it felt the same as someone drawing on my arm with a fine tip sharpie.
Third, the atmosphere is really nice. All the artists seem really nice and welcoming. The shop feels like a place of happy times with people being hyped about their new art or just hanging out with pals.
